         <iframe allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen="" class="embed-responsive-item" frameborder="0" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/Awo6-K4fpM8">
         </iframe>

        <figcaption class="figure-caption">
        </figcaption>
        <div class="h4-responsive">
         Deb Haaland Ceremonial Swearing-In
        </div>
        "History is being made yet again,"
        <a href="https://youtu.be/Awo6-K4fpM8">
         Vice President Kamala Harris said after administering a ceremonial oath of office to Deb Haaland, the new Secretary of the Interior. Haaland is the first Native person to lead the Department of the Interior and the first Native person
        </a>
        in a presidential cabinet.
       </div>

         <a href="https://www.indianz.com/covid19/2020/12/01/navajo-nation-arizona-new-mexico-utah-320/" title="Navajo Nation (Arizona, New Mexico, Utah)">
          Navajo Nation (Arizona, New Mexico, Utah)
         </a>
        </div>
        The total number of positive COVID-19 cases for the Navajo Nation is 16,595 as of November 30, 2020. Reports indicate 9,188 coronavirus recoveries on the largest reservation in the United States.
       </div>

  <script>
   function windowPopup(url, width, height) {
  // Calculate the position of the popup so
  // it’s centered on the screen.
  var left = (screen.width / 2) - (width / 2),
      top = (screen.height / 2) - (height / 2);

  window.open(
    url,
    "",
    "menubar=no,toolbar=no,resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes,width=" + width + ",height=" + height + ",top=" + top + ",left=" + left
  );
}
    
// Vanilla JavaScript
var jsSocialShares = document.querySelectorAll(".js-social-share");
if (jsSocialShares) {
  [].forEach.call(jsSocialShares, function(anchor) {
    anchor.addEventListener("click", function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();

      windowPopup(this.href, 500, 300);
    });
  });
}
  </script>
